/* Provide type definitions for commonly used types.
40
 *  These are useful because a "gint8" can be adjusted
41
 *  to be 1 byte (8 bits) on all platforms. Similarly and
42
 *  more importantly, "gint32" can be adjusted to be
43
 *  4 bytes (32 bits) on all platforms.
44
 */
45
46
typedef char   gchar;
47
typedef short  gshort;
48
typedef long   glong;
49
typedef int    gint;
50
typedef gint   gboolean;
51
52
typedef unsigned char   guchar;
53
typedef unsigned short  gushort;
54
typedef unsigned long   gulong;
55
typedef unsigned int    guint;
56
57
typedef float   gfloat;
58
typedef double  gdouble;
59

/* Define min and max constants for the fixed size numerical types */
61
/**
62
 * G_MININT8: (value -128)
63
 *
64
 * The minimum value which can be held in a #gint8.
65
 *
66
 * Since: 2.4
67
 */
68
#define G_MININT8 ((gint8) (-G_MAXINT8 - 1))
69
#define G_MAXINT8 ((gint8)  0x7f)
70
#define G_MAXUINT8  ((guint8) 0xff)
71
72
/**
73
 * G_MININT16: (value -32768)
74
 *
75
 * The minimum value which can be held in a #gint16.
76
 *
77
 * Since: 2.4
78
 */
79
#define G_MININT16  ((gint16) (-G_MAXINT16 - 1))
80
#define G_MAXINT16  ((gint16)  0x7fff)
81
#define G_MAXUINT16 ((guint16) 0xffff)
82
83
/**
84
 * G_MININT32: (value -2147483648)
85
 *
86
 * The minimum value which can be held in a #gint32.
87
 *
88
 * Since: 2.4
89
 */
90
#define G_MININT32  ((gint32) (-G_MAXINT32 - 1))
91
#define G_MAXINT32  ((gint32)  0x7fffffff)
92
#define G_MAXUINT32 ((guint32) 0xffffffff)
93
94
/**
95
 * G_MININT64: (value -9223372036854775808)
96
 *
97
 * The minimum value which can be held in a #gint64.
98
 */
99
#define G_MININT64  ((gint64) (-G_MAXINT64 - G_GINT64_CONSTANT(1)))
100
#define G_MAXINT64  G_GINT64_CONSTANT(0x7fffffffffffffff)
101
0
#define G_MAXUINT64 G_GUINT64_CONSTANT(0xffffffffffffffff)

/**
122
 * GCopyFunc:
123
 * @src: (not nullable): A pointer to the data which should be copied
124
 * @data: Additional data
125
 *
126
 * A function of this signature is used to copy the node data
127
 * when doing a deep-copy of a tree.
128
 *
129
 * Returns: (not nullable): A pointer to the copy
130
 *
131
 * Since: 2.4
132
 */
133
typedef gpointer  (*GCopyFunc)            (gconstpointer  src,
134
                                                 gpointer       data);
135
/**
136
 * GFreeFunc:
137
 * @data: a data pointer
138
 *
139
 * Declares a type of function which takes an arbitrary
140
 * data pointer argument and has no return value. It is
141
 * not currently used in GLib or GTK+.
142
 */
143
typedef void            (*GFreeFunc)            (gpointer       data);
144
145
/**
146
 * GTranslateFunc:
147
 * @str: the untranslated string
148
 * @data: user data specified when installing the function, e.g.
149
 *  in g_option_group_set_translate_func()
150
 * 
151
 * The type of functions which are used to translate user-visible
152
 * strings, for <option>--help</option> output.
153
 * 
154
 * Returns: a translation of the string for the current locale.
155
 *  The returned string is owned by GLib and must not be freed.
156
 */
157
typedef const gchar *   (*GTranslateFunc)       (const gchar   *str,
158
             gpointer       data);

/* Define some mathematical constants that aren't available
162
 * symbolically in some strict ISO C implementations.
163
 *
164
 * Note that the large number of digits used in these definitions
165
 * doesn't imply that GLib or current computers in general would be
166
 * able to handle floating point numbers with an accuracy like this.
167
 * It's mostly an exercise in futility and future proofing. For
168
 * extended precision floating point support, look somewhere else
169
 * than GLib.
170
 */
171

static inline gboolean _GLIB_CHECKED_ADD_U32 (guint32 *dest, guint32 a, guint32 b) {
472
  *dest = a + b; return *dest >= a; }
473
static inline gboolean _GLIB_CHECKED_MUL_U32 (guint32 *dest, guint32 a, guint32 b) {
474
  *dest = a * b; return !a || *dest / a == b; }
475
static inline gboolean _GLIB_CHECKED_ADD_U64 (guint64 *dest, guint64 a, guint64 b) {
476
  *dest = a + b; return *dest >= a; }
477
static inline gboolean _GLIB_CHECKED_MUL_U64 (guint64 *dest, guint64 a, guint64 b) {
478
  *dest = a * b; return !a || *dest / a == b; }
479
#endif
480
#endif /* __GTK_DOC_IGNORE__ */

/* IEEE Standard 754 Single Precision Storage Format (gfloat):
483
 *
484
 *        31 30           23 22            0
485
 * +--------+---------------+---------------+
486
 * | s 1bit | e[30:23] 8bit | f[22:0] 23bit |
487
 * +--------+---------------+---------------+
488
 * B0------------------->B1------->B2-->B3-->
489
 *
490
 * IEEE Standard 754 Double Precision Storage Format (gdouble):
491
 *
492
 *        63 62            52 51            32   31            0
493
 * +--------+----------------+----------------+ +---------------+
494
 * | s 1bit | e[62:52] 11bit | f[51:32] 20bit | | f[31:0] 32bit |
495
 * +--------+----------------+----------------+ +---------------+
496
 * B0--------------->B1---------->B2--->B3---->  B4->B5->B6->B7->
497
 */
498
/* subtract from biased_exponent to form base2 exponent (normal numbers) */
499
typedef union  _GDoubleIEEE754  GDoubleIEEE754;
500
typedef union  _GFloatIEEE754 GFloatIEEE754;
501
#define G_IEEE754_FLOAT_BIAS  (127)
502
#define G_IEEE754_DOUBLE_BIAS (1023)
503
/* multiply with base2 exponent to get base10 exponent (normal numbers) */
504
#define G_LOG_2_BASE_10   (0.30102999566398119521)
505
#if G_BYTE_ORDER == G_LITTLE_ENDIAN
506
union _GFloatIEEE754
507
{
508
  gfloat v_float;
509
  struct {
510
    guint mantissa : 23;
511
    guint biased_exponent : 8;
512
    guint sign : 1;
513
  } mpn;
514
};
515
union _GDoubleIEEE754
516
{
517
  gdouble v_double;
518
  struct {
519
    guint mantissa_low : 32;
520
    guint mantissa_high : 20;
521
    guint biased_exponent : 11;
522
    guint sign : 1;
523
  } mpn;
524
};
525
#elif G_BYTE_ORDER == G_BIG_ENDIAN
526
union _GFloatIEEE754
527
{
528
  gfloat v_float;
529
  struct {
530
    guint sign : 1;
531
    guint biased_exponent : 8;
532
    guint mantissa : 23;
533
  } mpn;
534
};
535
union _GDoubleIEEE754
536
{
537
  gdouble v_double;
538
  struct {
539
    guint sign : 1;
540
    guint biased_exponent : 11;
541
    guint mantissa_high : 20;
542
    guint mantissa_low : 32;
543
  } mpn;
544
};
545
#else /* !G_LITTLE_ENDIAN && !G_BIG_ENDIAN */
546
#error unknown ENDIAN type
547
#endif /* !G_LITTLE_ENDIAN && !G_BIG_ENDIAN */

#    ifdef GLIB_STATIC_COMPILATION
568
#      define GLIB_VAR extern
569
#    else /* !GLIB_STATIC_COMPILATION */
570
#      ifdef GLIB_COMPILATION
571
#        ifdef DLL_EXPORT
572
#          define GLIB_VAR __declspec(dllexport)
573
#        else /* !DLL_EXPORT */
574
#          define GLIB_VAR extern
575
#        endif /* !DLL_EXPORT */
576
#      else /* !GLIB_COMPILATION */
577
#        define GLIB_VAR extern __declspec(dllimport)
578
#      endif /* !GLIB_COMPILATION */
579
#    endif /* !GLIB_STATIC_COMPILATION */
580
#  else /* !G_PLATFORM_WIN32 */
581
#    define GLIB_VAR _GLIB_EXTERN
582
#  endif /* !G_PLATFORM_WIN32 */

#endif /* GLIB_VAR */
